}

	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/_thirdParty/contoso_example_ltd/adminPages/.gitkeep');

	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);

if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') != '55cd9f2712db762ebdbd7653940d69ec3daefda4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '55cd9f2712db762ebdbd7653940d69ec3daefda4') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '569a9faec1d4952ade44ae931f0d1de60ed81da8') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '55cd9f2712db762ebdbd7653940d69ec3daefda4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != '942481b69d7f2a78b422c87d9778ad486a0dcd5c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '942481b69d7f2a78b422c87d9778ad486a0dcd5c') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '97953be9c20c55837f2396d13c73c9d9a379eaf3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '942481b69d7f2a78b422c87d9778ad486a0dcd5c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	writefile_18();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') != '7bbc93a9a388667e370d101d9da939ef4444cab8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== '7bbc93a9a388667e370d101d9da939ef4444cab8') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== 'af8c9336aa97333a01fe3e488368328cdcd89e7f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_18();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== '7bbc93a9a388667e370d101d9da939ef4444cab8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html');
	writefile_20();
	if (!is_file('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html') != '4cfa01acc82daf53e43a8d7ae8c5fbc01cc93db8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html') !== '4cfa01acc82daf53e43a8d7ae8c5fbc01cc93db8') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html') !== '358e19d9b54fec16bace1f14228b6fdeb794fa23') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_20();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html') !== '4cfa01acc82daf53e43a8d7ae8c5fbc01cc93db8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/tutorial.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_21();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '8d290918eb2b0ad39c072d5aced73b06c848a30a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '8d290918eb2b0ad39c072d5aced73b06c848a30a') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '3e38733be7a39166a457ce8f9ca1960abc649ee6') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_21();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '8d290918eb2b0ad39c072d5aced73b06c848a30a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

}
if (!is_file('userdata/styles/info.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: userdata/styles/info.txt');
	writefile_23();
	if (!is_file('userdata/styles/info.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): userdata/styles/info.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('userdata/styles/info.txt') != 'f68e056e4f03ec3ab5ef85f5fdfaf737a71d3a4e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): userdata/styles/info.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('userdata/styles/info.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of userdata/styles/info.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('userdata/styles/info.txt') !== 'f68e056e4f03ec3ab5ef85f5fdfaf737a71d3a4e') {
		if (@sha1_file('userdata/styles/info.txt') !== '61e30b64da1e5dbe15a46eb6e0c5a864363a8b29') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: userdata/styles/info.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('userdata/styles/info.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('userdata/styles/info.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('userdata/styles/info.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_23();
		if (@sha1_file('userdata/styles/info.txt') !== 'f68e056e4f03ec3ab5ef85f5fdfaf737a71d3a4e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): userdata/styles/info.txt');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 632\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 632') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
